### [104] [The Role of Input Dimensionality in the Emergence and Targeted Control of Adversarial Examples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26207)
*Nasrin Malekzadeh Goradel,Niccolo Pancino,Yaser Gholizade Atani,Benedetta Tondi,Giovanni Bellettini,Mauro Barni*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了输入维度在对抗样本产生与目标控制中的作用，发现高维度使对抗样本更易构造，且目标攻击与无目标攻击的差距随维度增加而缩小，表明高输入维度是对抗脆弱性的根本因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论工作试图用高维几何解释深度神经网络的对抗脆弱性，但其假设缺乏系统的实证检验。本文旨在通过实验系统探究输入维度在对抗样本产生与目标控制中的实际作用。

Method: 1) 分析基于测度集中理论的理论框架的适用范围和局限性；2) 在跨输入维度的层次化图像数据集和多种神经网络架构上进行大规模实证评估；3) 通过理论论证和实验验证目标攻击与无目标攻击所需扰动差异随维度增加而减小的现象。

Result: 1) 真实图像类别表现出强经验局部化，超出理论假设范围；2) 对抗样本随维度增加更易构造；3) 高维几何使得目标攻击仅需比无目标攻击略大的扰动，且二者差距随维度增加而缩小。

Conclusion: 高输入维度是对抗样本产生和目标控制的根本因素，但其机制源于高维几何与数据分布的相互作用还是网络架构特性，仍有待进一步研究。

Abstract: Several theoretical works have tried to explain the adversarial vulnerability of deep neural networks through properties of high-dimensional geometry. However, the assumptions underlying these works are rarely examined empirically, and systematic evidence remains limited. In this work, we present a systematic study of the role of input dimensionality in both the emergence and the targeted control of adversarial examples. We first analyse the scope and limitations of existing theoretical frameworks based on concentration of measure, showing that real image classes exhibit strong empirical localization, beyond what such theories typically assume. We then conduct an extensive empirical evaluation across hierarchical image datasets spanning a wide range of input dimensionalities and diverse neural architectures. Our results consistently show that adversarial examples become easier to construct as dimensionality increases. We also investigate how input dimensionality affects the additional difficulty of crafting targeted adversarial examples. In particular, we provide theoretical arguments showing that high-dimensional geometry implies that enforcing a specific target label entails only a limited additional distortion compared to untargeted attacks. We corroborate this insight through extensive experiments, demonstrating that the gap between targeted and untargeted perturbations remains small and further narrows as input dimensionality increases. While, taken together, our findings establish high input dimensionality as a fundamental factor underlying the emergence and targeted control of adversarial examples, whether this phenomenon primarily arises from the interplay between high-dimensional geometry and data distributions or from the architectural properties of deep neural networks remains an open question.

</details>


### [105] [A probabilistic framework for online test-time adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26457)
*Daniel Corrales,David Ríos Insua*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于概率框架的在线测试时自适应方法，通过状态空间建模统一处理分布偏移下的参数学习、演化、先验调优与预测问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时自适应方法缺乏统一的概率视角，难以在理论上刻画参数随时间演化和分布偏移下的不确定性。

Method: 基于状态空间建模架构，将参数学习、参数时间演化、先验调优和预测纳入统一的概率框架中进行建模。

Result: 该框架能够系统性地处理训练与测试分布不一致时的在线自适应问题。

Conclusion: 提出的概率框架为在线测试时自适应提供了一种统一的理论基础。

Abstract: This paper presents a probabilistic framework for online test-time adaptation problems. In them, a model is trained on labeled data but must adapt to unlabeled data at test time under the assumption that training and test distributions potentially differ, that is, there might have been a distributional shift. The framework is based on a state-space modelling architecture from which parameter learning, parameter time evolution, prior tuning, and prediction can be characterized.

### [106] [XMSE-Aware Adaptive Empirical Bayes Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26975)
*Minghao Chen,Jiale Zheng*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种XMSE感知的混合估计器，在经验贝叶斯（EB）和最大似然估计（ML）之间进行插值，通过闭形式的最优混合权重实现风险不劣于两者，并证明了二阶后悔率界，仿真与基准实验验证了其在核匹配良好时保留正则化收益、核误配时退回到ML的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EB估计器虽在一阶渐近风险上可与ML匹敌，但在二阶风险（XMSE）分析中表现不佳——当核函数与真实参数对齐不良时，EB可能劣于ML。本文旨在将这一诊断转化为设计准则，构造一种能自适应调节、规避EB在核误配下风险的混合估计器。

Method: 提出XMSE感知的混合估计器，在ML与EB之间线性插值；推导固定权重下XMSE的标量二次形式，给出解析形式的最优插值权重；基于有限样本XMSE近似实现plug-in估计，证明其一致性及对内部最优权重的二阶后悔率；扩展至紧凑核族、有限/增长的核字典，并引入阈值边界规则。

Result: 理论证明所提估计器在XMSE尺度上不劣于ML和EB；plug-in估计达到二阶后悔率；仿真中针对SURE调参、硬选择、迹校正等基线，以及Silverbox和Cascaded Tanks基准，均显示在有利时保留正则化收益，核误配时退回ML。

Conclusion: XMSE感知的混合策略有效弥合了EB与ML之间的二阶风险差距，为核选择不确定场景下的稳健估计提供了一种理论上保证、实践中有效的方案。

Abstract: Empirical Bayes (EB) estimators can match the first-order asymptotic risk of maximum likelihood (ML) while behaving very differently at second order: recent excess mean squared error (XMSE) analysis shows that kernel-based EB estimation may be worse than ML when the kernel is poorly aligned with the true parameter. This paper turns that diagnostic into a design principle. We propose an XMSE-aware mixed estimator that interpolates between ML and EB shrinkage. Its fixed-weight XMSE is a scalar quadratic, yielding a closed-form oracle mixing weight that is no worse than both ML and the base EB estimator at the XMSE scale. A plug-in implementation based on finite-sample XMSE approximations is proved consistent, with a second-order oracle regret rate for an interior oracle weight. We further establish a transfer of the regret bound to the fixed-weight risk curve evaluated at the selected weight, a thresholded boundary rule, and extensions to compact kernel families and to finite and growing kernel dictionaries with high-probability oracle bounds. Finite impulse response simulations with SURE-tuned, hard-selection, and trace-corrected baselines, together with the public Silverbox and Cascaded Tanks benchmarks, show that the proposed estimator retains most of the benefit of regularization when it is helpful and retreats toward ML under kernel misspecification, with an identified finite-de analyzed on the benchmarks.

</details>


### [107] [Beyond Global Divergences: A Local-Mass Perspective on Bayesian Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27090)
*Hanli Xu,Fengxiang He,Sarat Moka*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究贝叶斯推断中全局目标（如KL散度、ELBO）无法捕捉的局部质量行为，引入质量指数（Mass Index）和正则化扩展KL（RE-KL）两种数学工具，从理论上刻画了局部质量在贝叶斯更新中的变化规律，并通过实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有贝叶斯推断方法（如KL散度、ELBO）关注全局分布差异，但无法刻画局部质量行为（例如在参数空间某点附近的概率质量衰减尺度）。本文旨在建立一套理论框架来定量分析和比较这种局部行为。

Method: (1) 提出**质量指数（Mass Index）**，用于记录局部质量的多项式和对数衰减尺度；(2) 提出**正则化扩展KL散度（RE-KL）**，一种可处理奇异成分的局部化散度；(3) 利用上述工具推导局部小球质量的绝对、相对和方向性不等式，从理论上刻画贝叶斯更新对局部质量的影响。

Result: (1) 质量指数可刻画：幂对数似然因子显式改变局部质量尺度，参数依赖支撑或其平滑软化可通过参数值附近保留的质量改变局部尺度；(2) 基于局部RE-KL证明了KL两个方向上局部小球质量的绝对、相对和方向性不等式；(3) 实验验证了理论结果。

Conclusion: 本文建立的局部质量理论框架弥补了全局目标（KL、ELBO）在局部行为刻画上的不足，为贝叶斯推断中局部质量行为提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: Global objectives, such as KL divergence and ELBO, are widely used in Bayesian inference for measuring distributional discrepancy. This paper studies their local-mass behaviour that is not directly captured by such objectives. We introduce and use two mathematical tools: (1) Mass Index for recording the polynomial and logarithmic decay scales of local mass, and (2) regularised extended KL (RE-KL), a set-localised divergence that can be formulated in the presence of singular components. Mass Indices help characterise how Bayesian updating changes local mass: (1) power-log likelihood factors shift it explicitly, and (2) parameter-dependent supports, or their smooth softenings, may change the local scale through the amount of mass that remains near the parameter value. Using local RE-KL, we prove absolute, relative, and directional inequalities for comparing local small-ball masses under the two KL directions. Together, these results provide a local theoretical account of local mass behaviour. Experiments provide controlled illustrations of the local behaviour. Code is available at https://github.com/Forsythia0604/Local-Mass-Framework.

</details>


### [108] [Ribbon: Scalable Approximation and Robust Uncertainty Quantification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27269)
*Graham Gibson,John Tipton,Kellin Rumsey,Natalie Klein*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: Ribbon 是一种通过影响函数线性化近似贝叶斯自助法的不确定性量化方法，只需单次模型拟合后的后验线性代数计算，避免了重复训练，在大规模模型上实现了高效且校准良好的不确定性估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的贝叶斯方法和自助重采样方法虽然能提供可靠的不确定性估计，但对于现代机器学习模型（复杂、高维、可能误设定）而言，需要后验采样或重复模型拟合，计算成本过高。

Method: 通过影响函数线性化，在单个拟合模型周围进行一阶近似，保留贝叶斯自助法的数据重加权结构，只需后验线性代数计算即可近似狄利克雷重加权自助法的不确定性。

Result: 在合成回归、MNIST分类和加州房价基准上，Ribbon 提供了具有竞争力的预测性能和更好的校准效果，同时避免了重复模型训练。

Conclusion: Ribbon 在理论上与平坦先验拉普拉斯近似渐近等价（在正确似然设定下），在误设定下恢复稳健三明治协方差，是一种兼具理论保证和实际效率的不确定性量化方法。

Abstract: Reliably quantifying predictive uncertainty is difficult for complex, high-dimensional, or misspecified models. Both fully Bayesian and bootstrap resampling methods provide principled uncertainty estimates but are often too expensive for modern machine-learning models because they require posterior sampling or repeated model refitting. We introduce Ribbon, a scalable approximation to Dirichlet-reweighted bootstrap uncertainty. Ribbon replaces repeated refitting with an influence-function linearization around a single fitted model, preserving the first-order data-reweighting structure of the Bayesian bootstrap while requiring only post-hoc linear algebra. Ribbon approximates the Bayesian-bootstrap or weighted-likelihood-bootstrap refitting target. With a general concentration parameter, Ribbon gives a calibrated Dirichlet-reweighting family whose uncertainty scale can be tuned on validation data. We show that Ribbon is asymptotically equivalent to a flat-prior Laplace approximation under correct likelihood specification and recovers the robust sandwich covariance under misspecification. Across synthetic regression, MNIST classification, and California Housing benchmarks, Ribbon provides competitive predictive performance and improved calibration in several settings while avoiding repeated model retraining.

</details>


### [109] [When are likely answers right? On Sequence Probability and Correctness in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27359)
*Johannes Zenn,Jonas Geiping*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了序列概率与生成正确性之间的关系，发现在数据集内更高概率的答案往往更正确，但在解码方法或超参数层面提升概率并不总能提升正确率，且同一提示下的多次响应中概率不能可靠指示正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多LLM解码方法通过提升序列概率来改进输出，但序列概率与正确性之间的关系并不明确，作者希望系统量化这一关系。

Method: 在四个层面（解码方法间、超参数间、数据集内提示-答案对间、同一提示的多次响应间）进行实验分析，比较序列概率与正确性的关联。

Result: 数据集内更高概率的答案通常更正确；但改变解码方法或超参数来提升概率并不稳定地提升正确率；同一提示的多次响应中，概率不能可靠指示正确性。

Conclusion: 澄清了序列概率在何种情况下能/不能作为正确性的可靠指标，为解码、自一致性及无验证器自我改进提供了实践指导。

Abstract: Many decoding methods for large language models can be understood as shifting probability mass toward outputs that are more likely under the model, either locally at the token level or globally at the sequence level. Therefore, their success depends on a fundamental question: when does sequence probability, that is, the conditional probability of a continuation given a prompt, actually align with correctness? In this paper, we set out to quantify this relationship across decoding methods, models, and benchmarks at four levels: across decoding methods, across hyperparameters within a method, across prompt-answer pairs within a dataset, and across repeated responses to the same prompt. We find that higher sequence probability is often predictive of correctness across prompt-answer pairs within a fixed dataset. However, this relationship does not generally transfer to decoding decisions: increasing sequence probability by changing hyperparameters or methods does not reliably improve accuracy. Further, sequence probability is not a good indicator of correctness for responses to the same prompt. These findings clarify when decoding can and cannot be expected to improve correctness, and provide practical guidance for decoding, self-consistency, and verifier-free self-improvement.

</details>

### [110] [Benchmarking Open-Weight Foundation Models for Global AI Technical Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26099)
*Jason Hung*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究通过使用开源大模型和细粒度分类方法，克服了以往研究在评估AI地理偏见时的三大方法论缺陷，发现模型对训练数据中代表性不足的国家存在显著的准确性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在AI治理分析中广泛应用，但存在地理偏见——对训练数据中代表性不足的国家回答准确性显著降低。此前研究存在三大方法论局限：依赖闭源模型无法复现、评估年份超出模型知识范围、使用粗粒度二元分类无法区分模型是自信编造还是诚实承认无知。本研究旨在通过改进方法学来克服这些局限。

Method: 使用四个开源权重前沿语言模型，基于Global AI Dataset v2（GAID v2）基准数据集，选取18个指标对应IEEE IRAI 2026框架的八个维度，约2,990个国别-指标-年份观测值，时间跨度为2010-2023年。采用五分类方案（VA, HF, HR, QH, MF）对模型回答进行分类，通过混合效应逻辑回归和双重差分分析（DiD）估计地理差异。

Result: 通过五分类方案能够区分模型自信编造（HF）与诚实承认不确定性（HR），并且通过混合效应逻辑回归和双重差分分析揭示了模型在不同地理区域间的准确性差异。

Conclusion: 通过克服三大方法论局限，本研究的发现更加可靠。开源模型和细粒度分类方法为未来AI地理偏见研究提供了可复现的评估框架。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in artificial intelligence (AI) governance analysis across national and international organisations. There is, however, growing evidence that such models produce significantly less accurate responses for countries that are underrepresented in their training data-a pattern described in existing literature as geographic bias. Existing studies examining this phenomenon are subject to three methodological limitations that together undermine their findings: (1) reliance on proprietary systems whose weights are not publicly released, which prevents independent replication; (2) evaluation of model knowledge about years that fall after data collection for model training had concluded, leading to geographic ignorance in addition to the natural limits of each model's knowledge; and (3) use of coarse binary response classification that cannot distinguish models' confident fabrication (HF) from their honest acknowledgement of uncertainty. This study addresses all three limitations by benchmarking four open-weight frontier language models against the Global AI Dataset v2 (GAID v2), a verified ground-truth database of 24,453 indicators across 227 countries published on Harvard Dataverse in January 2026. A total of 18 indicators, mapped to the eight thematic dimensions of the IEEE IRAI 2026 framework, are selected from GAID v2, yielding approximately 2,990 country-metric-year observations across six evaluation years (within the period of 2010-2023). Model responses are classified using a five-category scheme that distinguishes (a) verified accuracy (VA), (b) HF, (c) honest refusal (HR), (d) qualitative hedging (QH), and (e) misattribution (MF). Geographic disparities in accuracy are estimated through mixed-effects logistic regression and difference-in-differences (DiD) analysis.

</details>


### [111] [Simulating Eating Disorder Patients with LLMs: Evaluating Psychological Persona Stability in Multi-Turn Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26109)
*Jennifer Haase,Jana Gonnermann-Müller,See Heng Yim,Nicolas Leins,Jan Mendling,Sebastian Pokutta*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 基于LLM的临床患者模拟在人格稳定性上存在悖论：模型在对话间和对话内表现出过高的稳定性（几乎无方差），但系统性高估进食障碍严重程度（12-30%），存在“选择性刻板印象”——行为项目能区分病例，但认知-情感项目始终达到天花板效应，导致“中间缺失”现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证基于LLM的临床患者模拟是否满足人格稳定性（即连贯维持指定心理特征）这一前提条件，从而评估其在研究和训练中的有效性。

Method: 使用五个已发表案例小传构建进食障碍人格，采用自评+独立观察者双评估框架，结合已知真实值的EDE-Q量表。在六个LLM上进行两次实验（对话间稳定性Exp.I和对话内稳定性Exp.II）。

Result: 所有模型变异可忽略不计（过于稳定），但系统性高估真实严重程度12-30%（0.7-1.8分/6分制）。机制是选择性刻板印象：行为项目（饮食限制）能区分病例，但认知-情感项目（身体不满、体重先占）无论病例严重程度均达到天花板。更多对话上下文反而加剧高估。

Conclusion: LLM能够描绘严重的进食病理，但缺乏对中度临床表现的表征能力，存在“中间缺失”问题，表明当前模型在模拟温和或中等程度临床病例方面存在根本性局限。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM)-based simulations of clinical patients are increasingly used for research and training, yet their validity requires persona stability: coherent maintenance of an assigned psychological profile across and within conversations. We evaluate this prerequisite using eating disorder personas grounded in five published case vignettes, a dual-assessment framework (self-report + independent observer ratings), and validated psychometric instruments (EDE-Q) with known ground-truth scores. Across six LLMs and two experiments (between-conversation stability (Exp. I) and within-conversation stability (Exp. II)), we find that LLMs are paradoxically too stable and too inaccurate: variability is negligible, yet all models systematically overshoot ground-truth severity by 12-30% of the scale range (0.7-1.8 points on a 0-6 scale). The mechanism is selective stereotyping: models differentiate cases on behavioural items (dietary restraint) but maximise cognitive-affective items (body dissatisfaction, weight preoccupation) at ceiling regardless of case severity. Additional conversational context does not improve accuracy; it compounds the overshoot. LLMs can portray severe eating pathology but lack a representation of moderate clinical presentations, a "missing middle".

</details>


### [112] [Generative AI and Copyright Infringement: A Legal-Technical Analysis of AI Music Generation Systems Under 17 U.S.C. Title 17](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26111)
*Zuhaib Hussain Butt*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文分析了GenAI音乐创作（如Google Gemini）在美国版权法下的法律风险，指出歌词复制构成侵权，AI模仿声音主要涉及州级形象权而非联邦版权，并揭示了联邦法律对合成声音保护不足的监管漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着GenAI工具（如Gemini）允许用户通过文本提示合成音乐（结合受版权保护的歌词、AI作曲、模仿真实艺术家声音），现有法律框架（联邦版权法、州形象权法）对这类新型创作行为的适用性存在重大不确定性，亟需系统分析。

Method: 整合Title 17版权法（复制权、衍生作品权、发行权）、17 U.S.C. §114（声音录音的窄保护）、新兴州级声音克隆法案，并结合近期案例（Concord v. Anthropic, Kadrey v. Meta, Lehrman v. Lovo等）进行法律分析；同时将AI技术组件（提示编码、潜扩散、神经声码器、说话人嵌入）映射至具体法律风险。

Result: ①未经授权的歌词复制构成高侵权风险；②AI声音模仿通常不在联邦录音保护范围内，主要涉及州形象权；③识别出监管漏洞：联邦法律对歌词和旋律提供强保护，但对合成声音相似性的救济不足。

Conclusion: 建议为AI音乐创作制定更清晰的监管规则，填补对合成人声的法律保护空白。

Abstract: Generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) has enabled users to synthesize music with text prompts, combining copyrighted lyrics, AI-composed melodies, and synthetic vocals that imitate real artists. This paper examines the legal and technical dimensions of AI-based music creation (e.g., Google Gemini's music tools) under U.S. copyright law. We analyze whether a user who inputs one artist's protected lyrics into a GenAI system, directs it to use another artist's voice or style, publishes the resulting song, and monetizes it violates 17 U.S.C. Section 106's exclusive rights [3]. The analysis integrates Title 17 doctrine (rights of reproduction, derivative works, distribution), 17 U.S.C. Section 114's narrow sound recording protection [4], and the new voice-cloning laws emerging at the state level [20].
  We argue that unauthorized lyric copying poses a high risk of infringement of the musical composition, whereas mere AI-generated voice imitation typically falls outside federal sound recording protection and instead implicates state publicity rights [12], [13]. Recent cases and legislation (Concord v. Anthropic [10]; Kadrey v. Meta [11]; Lehrman v. Lovo [12]; Tennessee's "ELVIS Act" [20]; UMG v. Uncharted Labs [14]; etc.) illustrate this split. We map AI technical components (prompt encoding, latent diffusion, neural vocoders, speaker embeddings) to legal risks and identify a regulatory gap: federal law robustly protects lyrics and melody but currently provides limited remedies for synthesized vocal likeness [22], [23]. The paper concludes with policy suggestions for clearer rules on AI music creation.

Abstract: We examine the structural transformation of creative industries under generative artificial intelligence, drawing on 374 primary sources spanning policy documents, industry data, creator surveys, and platform analytics. Abstract: This paper proposes a multi-layer AI framework for information landscape analysis in the context of information disorder. The goal is to move beyond isolated claim verification toward a structured representation of the informational environment surrounding an event, entity, or narrative. We argue that AI systems for media analysis should support epistemic mapping: a transparent, multi-dimensional account of how facts, interpretations, actors, and narratives interact over time. The paper presents the conceptual architecture, analytical layers, and methodological rationale of the framework, with the aim of supporting more nuanced, explainable, and critically useful tools for information disorder research.

### [115] [Divergent Recommendations, Convergent Diagnoses: Cross-Provider Failure-Mode Convergence in AI Commercial Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26116)
*Will Jack,Noah Lehman,Keller Maloney,Sarah Xu*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 当ChatGPT和Claude在品牌推荐上有约2/3的分歧时，它们在诊断品牌为何未被推荐的原因上却高度一致（95.1%），尤其是在长尾品牌上（99.6%），这为品牌优化提供了差异化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究两个主流大语言模型（ChatGPT和Claude）在品牌推荐上的一致性程度，以及当品牌未被推荐时，两个模型对失败原因的诊断是否一致，从而为品牌方制定跨平台优化策略提供依据。

Method: 在四个测量批次中收集215个商业化框架提示，比较两个模型推荐品牌的Jaccard相似度；对于未被推荐的品牌，将失败分为三种模式（可发现性、吸引力、定位），并计算两个模型诊断一致率。

Result: 两个模型推荐品牌的分歧很大（Jaccard 0.35），但诊断失败模式的一致率高达95.1%；一致性随品牌知名度下降而上升，从类别领先者的81%到长尾品牌的99.6%。

Conclusion: 品牌方应针对长尾品牌采取统一的失败模式修复策略（跨平台有效），而对类别领先者则需采取平台特定的内容层优化。

Abstract: A brand whose customers use both ChatGPT and Claude for product recommendations faces a strategic choice: a single optimization playbook, or one per provider? Across 215 commercially-framed prompts in four measurement batches, the two providers disagree on which brands they recommend roughly two-thirds of the time (cross-provider recommendation Jaccard 0.35, below the 0.50-0.61 same-prompt rerun baseline). The picks diverge. But when neither provider recommends a brand, we classify the failure into one of three modes -- discoverability (the brand never reaches the model), compellingness (it reaches the model but isn't mentioned), or positioning (it's mentioned but not recommended) -- and on 7,763 such joint failures, both providers diagnose the same failure mode 95.1% of the time (clustered 95% CI [94.3%, 95.7%]). Agreement rises monotonically with falling brand prominence, from 81% [78.2%, 84.0%] on category leaders to 99.6% [99.3%, 99.9%] on long-tail regional brands. The two providers reach their picks by measurably different generative routes -- Anthropic recommends from priors 43-52% of the time, OpenAI 8-29% -- but they converge on the failure diagnosis where it matters most for the long tail. Work that addresses the diagnosed failure mode lifts visibility on both providers; positioning - and content-level work for category leaders is more provider-specific.

### [116] [The Governance Inversion Hypothesis: Why More AI Regulation May Produce Less Organisational Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26117)
*Victor Frimpong*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出"治理倒置假说"（GIH），指出在AI治理中，监管扩张与制度复杂化可能导致组织表面治理增强、实际控制力削弱的悖论，并通过四个机制（权威碎片化、象征性治理扩张、控制外部化、权威瘫痪）解释这一现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI治理框架普遍假设更强监管能提升问责与组织控制，但本文质疑这一假设，旨在揭示治理形式化本身可能侵蚀对AI系统的实际控制能力。

Method: 基于制度理论、组织治理研究、问责制学术及新兴AI治理文献，构建概念性框架，提出四个相互关联的机制来解释治理扩张如何削弱操作控制。

Result: 发现治理系统日益层级化与程序化后，组织可能难以维持一致的权威、技术可见性、升级能力及对不透明AI基础设施的有效干预权力。

Conclusion: AI治理的核心风险不是缺乏治理结构，而是出现"看似被治理、实则丧失治理能力"的制度性悖论；文章扩展了制度解耦理论，提出"治理倒置"作为结构性条件。

Abstract: This paper introduces the Governance Inversion Hypothesis (GIH) to explain a growing paradox in artificial intelligence (AI) governance: under conditions of increasing regulatory expansion and technological complexity, organisations may become more formally governed while simultaneously experiencing a decline in operational control over AI systems. Existing AI governance frameworks generally assume that stronger regulation improves accountability, oversight, and organisational control. This paper challenges that assumption by arguing that governance formalisation itself may contribute to the erosion of control in AI-intensive environments. Drawing on institutional theory, organisational governance research, accountability scholarship, and emerging AI governance literature, the paper develops a conceptual framework explaining how regulatory expansion may weaken operational authority through four interconnected mechanisms: authority fragmentation, symbolic governance expansion, externalisation of control, and authority paralysis. As governance systems become increasingly layered and procedurally dense, organisations may struggle to maintain coherent authority, technical visibility, escalation capability, and meaningful intervention power over opaque and externally mediated AI infrastructures. The paper extends institutional decoupling theory by introducing governance inversion as a structural condition in which governance expansion may actively undermine operational coherence rather than strengthen it. It concludes that the central risk in AI governance may not be the absence of governance structures, but the emergence of institutions that appear increasingly governed while progressively losing the capacity to govern effectively.

### [118] [The Effortless Trap: Productive Struggle, AI, and the Illusion of Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26181)
*Mario Brcic,Stjepan Frljic*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文提出“允许还是禁止AI”是错误二分法，关键在于AI的“放置”位置。作者提出六步学习模型（Prime, Probe, Point, Attach, Strengthen, Test），强调保护首次努力尝试和最终无辅助测试，中间用有防护的AI辅助。若AI让任务变得毫不费力，则放置错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI发展迅速，教育者对“允许还是禁止AI”感到困惑，因为AI既可能帮助学习也可能损害学习。作者认为这种二元对立是虚假的，需要转换问题框架。

Method: 提出六步学习模型（Prime, Probe, Point, Attach, Strengthen, Test），以及放置规则（保护首次努力和最终测试，中间用防护性AI辅助），并映射经典教学策略和AI干预措施到每个步骤。

Result: 因果证据表明：无防护的AI助手让高中生在无辅助考试中比不使用工具的学生差约17%；同一模型通过重建以保留答案消除了危害；精心设计的AI导学工具则使学习效果翻倍。

Conclusion: 六步模型、放置规则和干预菜单为AI时代课程与教学设计提供了实用基础。

Abstract: With AI advancing fast, educators face a dilemma: allow the tool or ban it. Conflicting evidence that it both helps and hurts learning only deepens the confusion. The allow-or-ban framing is a false dichotomy; the relevant design question is placement. Used well, AI can scale feedback, examples, practice, and individualized support. Used poorly, it replaces the cognitive work that learning requires and leaves an illusion of learning: a confident sense of mastery that collapses on the unaided task. The strongest causal evidence shows the outcome flips on design: an unguarded AI helper left high-school students about 17% worse on an unaided exam than peers with no tool at all, while the same model rebuilt to withhold answers erased the harm, and a well-engineered tutor roughly doubled learning. We give educators one graspable frame for placing the tool. A new idea is learned through six moves, in order: Prime, Probe, Point, Attach, Strengthen, and Test. Secure the first hard attempt and the final unaided check, scaffold with guarded AI in between, and one diagnostic carries the frame: if letting AI in makes the task feel effortless, it is in the wrong place. To make it usable, we map classical teaching moves and AI-supported interventions to each step. Together, the six-move model, the placement rule, and the intervention menu provide a practical foundation for lesson and course redesign in the age of AI.

### [119] [Enterprise Data Asset Quality: A Management-Standard Conformity-Benefit Realization Framework and Formation Mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26186)
*Yixuan Zhu,Aian Wu,Runhan Zhang,Xiyi Wang,Junfeng Yu,Aihua Han*

Main category: cs.CY

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用混合方法：基于扎根理论和LDA主题建模构建三维框架；PLS-SEM分析净效应；NCA分析必要条件；fsQCA分析组态路径。

Result: 三个维度间存在显著正向关系，数据资产管理能力对数据质量标准化符合度影响最强，并形成"管理基础→标准提升→价值实现"的链式机制；三个维度均是实现高数据资产质量的关键必要条件；识别出治理导向型和收益驱动型等多条等效组态路径。

Abstract: Motivated by the limited standardization of enterprise data asset quality evaluation and the unclear relationship between assessment outcomes and value realization, this study develops a three-dimensional framework comprising Data Asset Management Capability, Data Quality Standard Conformity, and Data Asset Benefit Realization Capability, based on grounded theory and LDA topic modeling. To examine the formation mechanisms of data asset quality, this study adopts a multi-method approach combining PLS-SEM, Necessary Condition Analysis (NCA), and fuzzy-set Qualitative Comparative Analysis (fsQCA), to capture net effects, capability thresholds, and configurational paths. The results show that significant positive relationships exist among the three dimensions, with Data Asset Management Capability exerting the strongest effect on Data Quality Standard Conformity and further promoting Data Asset Benefit Realization Capability, forming a chain mechanism of management foundation-standard enhancement-value realization. In addition, all three dimensions constitute critical necessary conditions for achieving high data asset quality, and multiple equivalent configurational paths reflecting different combinations of Management, Standard, and Benefit are identified, such as governance-oriented and benefit-driven mechanisms. This study integrates structural (PLS-SEM), necessary-condition (NCA), and configurational (fsQCA) analyses within a unified framework, providing a systematic approach to understanding data asset quality formation and offering practical insights for enterprise data governance and data factor market development.

</details>


### [120] [The Tilted Playing Field for Women in Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26469)
*Casandra Rusti,Hussain Hussain,Kian Ahrabian,Jay Pujara,Allon G. Percus,Buddhika Nettasinghe,Kristina Lerman*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文基于近500万篇论文和650万作者的数据，发现科研机构的声望优势并非性别中立：女性仅在顶尖机构才能获得与男性相当的声望回报，而男性在整个机构层级中持续受益，且差距在高成就者中进一步扩大。声望优势非线性增长，与性别差异化的合作网络结构密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究科研机构声望是否对研究者产生不平等的回报，以及这种声望优势如何与性别、生产力、合作模式相关联，揭示科学界是否存在不平等的竞争环境。

Method: 基于近500万篇论文、650万作者、超过6.5万个机构的数据，采用分布性、尾部敏感的分析框架，量化不同性别和机构层级下声望优势的差异，并结合合作网络结构分析。

Result: 男性在整个机构层级中持续享有声望优势，而女性仅在顶尖机构才能获得同等回报；声望优势非线性增长，集中于精英机构；高成就者中性别差距进一步扩大；女性合作网络更本地化，男性跨机构合作更广泛。

Conclusion: 科学界的声望优势并非性别中立，而是与性别和合作网络结构密切相关，揭示了不平等的竞争环境（"倾斜的赛场"）。

Abstract: Institutional prestige shapes access to resources, visibility, and collaboration opportunities in science. Yet whether prestige benefits researchers equally, and how it relates to differences in scientific productivity and collaboration, remains unclear. Here, we quantify prestige advantage as the relative likelihood that researchers at higher-ranked institutions have more collaborators and produce more high-impact papers compared to their lower-ranked peers. Analyzing nearly 5 million papers by 6.5 million authors across more than 65,000 institutions, we present a distributional, tail-sensitive framework to compare prestige advantage across groups. We find that the association between prestige and scientific achievement differs systematically by gender. While both men and women benefit from prestige, the returns are not gender-neutral: women experience comparable advantages only at the most elite institutions, whereas men retain persistent advantages across the broader hierarchy, with disparities widening at higher levels of achievement. Prestige advantage also grows nonlinearly, disproportionately benefiting authors at the most elite institutions. These differences align with collaboration patterns: women's networks are more locally clustered and focused on their own institution, while men collaborate more broadly across institutional strata. Together, these findings reveal a tilted playing field in science: one where prestige amplifies success unevenly and network structure shapes who can access its benefits.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Thought leadership plays a crucial role in boosting team performance; thus, teams with more thought leaders may perform better. However, the impact of the number of thought leaders on team performance in a scientific context remains understudied. Leveraging more than 140,000 papers from PLOS journals, we examine the relationship between the number of thought leaders and two aspects of team performance, namely team impact and team disruptiveness, from both correlational and causal perspectives. The results show that (1) an inverted U-shaped relationship exists between the number of thought leaders and team impact, and (2) teams with more thought leaders tend to produce less disruptive ideas. We also explore how international collaboration, team size, and gender diversity interact with the number of thought leaders in shaping team performance, and find that (3) international collaboration improves team impact but lowers the disruptiveness of team outputs. This study advances scholarly understanding of thought leadership in scientific teams and provides valuable insights for policymakers and team managers.

### [122] [Pingquanqi (Equalizer): A Cross-Domain Sociotechnical Framework for Human-Agent Interaction Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26573)
*Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 提出Pingquanqi（均衡器）框架，一种跨领域社会技术规范，旨在通过四个集成组件（用户状态判别、贝叶斯止损、可控摩擦、Lsteal透明度指标）优化LLM Agent从物理资本到用户生命周期的成本链，解决人机交互中的"寿命泄漏"问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM Agent正从实验工具转变为永久性基础设施，如同电网一样承载成本链（物理资本→企业投资→用户消费→用户寿命）。当前该成本链存在"泄漏"，未优化的交互消耗用户生命周期而未给予充分补偿，亟需一套治理框架来量化并控制这种隐性成本。

Method: 提出Pingquanqi框架，包含四个核心组件：①用户状态判别模型（主动知识水平适配）；②贝叶斯渐进式止损规则（限制单次交互成本）；③可控摩擦机制（打破自我强化的依赖循环）；④Lsteal透明度指标（将Token消耗转化为用户生命周期成本的可视化度量）。另增第五机制F5反思性摘要（引导认知回顾）。哲学基础融合毛泽东思想（实践论）、王阳明（知行合一）和黑格尔（理论与实践统一）。

Result: 框架以Agent框架层嵌入式设计规范的形式呈现（类比WCAG），可作为原生中间件部署。主要经济效益归于部署Agent服务的企业（减少计算浪费、提升用户满意度、维持订阅收入），用户受益为下游自然结果。

Conclusion: Pingquanqi的目标是成为一种被采纳的标准而非被购买的产品，通过标准化人机交互治理，在保护用户生命周期的同时实现企业经济效益，体现了跨文化哲学的融合与实用性。

Abstract: LLM agents are transitioning from experimental tools to permanent infrastructure -- a computational layer as enduring as the electrical grid. Like any infrastructure, they carry a cost chain from physical capital through enterprise investment to user consumption, ending at the user's most irreplaceable resource: lifetime. When unoptimized, this chain leaks, consuming user lifetime without adequate compensation. This paper proposes Pingquanqi (Equalizer), a cross-domain sociotechnical framework for Human-Agent Interaction Governance (HAIGF). Its product form is an Agent framework-level embedded design specification, analogous to WCAG for web accessibility, whose goal is not to be purchased but adopted as a standard. Pingquanqi consists of four integrated components deployable as native middleware: (1) a user-state discrimination model enabling proactive knowledge leveling, (2) a Bayesian progressive stop-loss rule capping per-session interaction cost, (3) controlled friction mechanisms breaking self-reinforcing dependency loops, and (4) Lsteal, a transparency metric rendering token-to-lifetime cost conversion visible. A fifth mechanism, reflective summarization (F5), enables guided cognitive recollection. The framework is grounded in cross-cultural philosophy: Mao's epistemology of practice (On Practice, 1937) provides the basis for cross-session knowledge accumulation; Wang Yangming's unity of knowledge and action (zhi xing he yi, c. 1509) illuminates Lsteal's root -- knowing without acting is incomplete; and Hegel's unity of theory and practice demonstrates cross-traditional convergence. This paper argues Pingquanqi's primary economic beneficiary is the enterprise deploying Agent services -- through reduced wasted computation, improved user satisfaction, and sustained subscription revenue -- with individual user benefit as the natural downstream consequence.

</details>


### [123] [Human--LLM Collaboration Is Transforming Complexity Metrics in Scientific Texts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27052)
*R. Alexander Bentley,Blai Vidiella,Damian J. Ruck,Senjuti Dutta,Kai Li,Sergi Valverde*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本研究利用复杂性科学方法，分析了2010-2025年间数百万篇arXiv摘要，发现2023年LLM广泛使用后，科学文本的涌现属性发生了微妙但可检测的变化：高频词更替率显著上升，LLM相关风格指数与词汇丰富度指标的正相关关系趋于平缓。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM正迅速成为语言生态系统的参与者，可能改变语言的涌现属性，尤其当模型越来越多地使用混合人机文本进行训练时。研究旨在检测这种变化的早期信号。

Method: 以2023年LLM的广泛使用为自然实验分界点，分析arXiv摘要中：1) LLM关联风格指数；2) Zipf定律和Heaps定律的指数；3) 高频词更替率；4) 风格指数与复杂性指标的关系变化。

Result: 2023年后：1) LLM风格指数急剧上升；2) Zipf和Heaps定律指数变化微弱；3) 高频词更替率显著增加；4) LLM风格指数与词汇量、Heaps指数、Zipf指数的正相关关系趋于平缓。

Conclusion: 这些模式表明，在人机混合语言生态系统中，科学文本的涌现属性正在发生变化，LLM的影响虽微妙但可被检测到。

Abstract: While human language has long been studied as a complex system, Large Language Models (LLMs) are rapidly becoming contributors to its dynamics. Because LLMs are trained on human language use, their effects on the broader human-AI linguistic ecosystem are likely subtle at first. As their use becomes more widespread, however, LLMs may alter emergent properties of language, particularly as models increasingly train on mixed human-LLM textual data. Here, we draw on complexity science to look for subtle LLM effects in millions of arXiv abstracts from 2010 to 2025. The year 2023, when LLMs rapidly became widely used, serves as a landmark in a natural experiment. While we find a sharp increase in a composite LLM-associated style index after early 2023, we observe only subtle changes in the exponents of Zipf's law and Heaps' law. More compelling, however, are two subtle changes in complexity metrics that emerge from 2023 onward. First, turnover among top-ranked words increases sharply. Second, the positive relationship between the LLM-associated style index and three complexity metrics--vocabulary size and the exponents of Heaps' and Zipf's laws--becomes flatter after 2022. Together, these patterns are consistent with changes in the emergent properties of scientific text in a mixed human-AI linguistic ecosystem.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对匿名内容社区进行大规模实证研究，识别并分析了24,105个AI生成的合成非自愿色情内容项目。

Result: 发现目标人口结构显著变化：非名人占比从4.7%升至55.8%；开源模型主导生产（Stable Diffusion占图像42.7%，Wan占视频66.5%）；少数活跃生产者（单人最多产出780项）驱动社区参与、塑造目标人口并传播技术知识。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了AI脱衣生态系统的运作机制，强调需要在平台治理、技术防护和受害者保护方面采取紧急干预措施。

Abstract: AI nudification uses generative models to create synthetic non-consensual sexually explicit imagery (SNEACI) of real individuals. However, the anonymous content community, where SNEACI is actively requested, generated, and exchanged, remains unexplored. In this work, we present a large-scale study of AI nudification in the wild, identifying 24,105 SNEACI items. We find a significant shift in target demographics: non-celebrity individuals now account for 55.8\% of targets, compared to only 4.7\% in prior studies, indicating that AI nudification has expanded from targeting public figures to increasingly harming individuals within users' own social circles. Meanwhile, open-source models dominate production, with Stable Diffusion family generating 42.7\% of images and Wan generating 66.5\% of videos, all driven by thousands of shared fine-tuned models and accessible tutorials. Yet the ecosystem runs on a small cohort of active producers, with the most prolific producing 780 items, drives community engagement, shapes target demographics, and disseminates technical knowledge that lowers barriers for new producers. Our work provides an empirical understanding of how AI nudification operates in the wild, revealing the mechanisms that sustain this ecosystem and highlighting the urgent need for interventions in platform governance, technical safeguards, and affected individual protection.

### [125] [Detecting and Controlling Sycophancy with Cascading Linear Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26155)
*Maty Bohacek,Rishub Jain,Nicholas Dufour,Thomas Leung,Chris Bregler,Roma Patel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种迭代式数据生成流程，通过构造级联样本（反映行为线性缩放的特征）替代简单二元对比样本，更好地解耦和发现模型中的谄媚行为特征，实现低计算成本、高可解释性的检测和干预。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的激活引导（activation steering）方法依赖大量二元对比样本来发现行为相关特征，但二元对比样本难以有效解耦复杂行为中的线性特征，导致特征发现和模型操控效果受限。

Method: 提出了一种迭代式数据生成流水线：逐步生成体现行为程度变化的级联样本（cascading samples），捕捉随行为线性缩放的特征，从而更好地分离与谄媚行为相关的特征子空间。

Result: 级联样本发现的谄媚特征形成了线性可分的子空间；在检测、确定性评分和稳健操控上匹配或优于LLM-as-a-judge和系统提示基线，同时计算成本更低、可解释性更强。

Conclusion: 超越简单二元对比，构造反映特征线性缩放关系的级联样本能显著提升特征解耦效果，为模型行为的可解释性分析和可控干预提供了更高效、更可靠的方案。

Abstract: Interpreting and controlling model behaviors through activation steering methods requires many pairs of contrastive samples that clearly exhibit desired or undesired behavior. These data pairs determine the degree to which interpretability frameworks can reliably detect model features responsible for a behavior, and therefore the ability to steer models toward or away from such behavior. In this work, we present an iterative data generation pipeline that isolates cascading linear features responsible for a behavior. Specifically, we show how moving beyond simple binary pairs of samples, and instead isolating samples that show degrees of features that scale linearly with behavior, allows for better disentanglement of features. We focus on detecting and steering away from sycophancy -- the tendency of language models to prioritize user validation. We demonstrate that sycophancy features discovered through cascading samples form linearly separable subspaces, and allow for selection of model activations that more clearly correspond to the desired behavior than baseline approaches. We also evaluate their ability to enable detection, deterministic scoring, and robust steering, and see that they either match or outperform LLM-as-a-judge and system prompting baselines while providing lower computational demand and more interpretability guarantees. Code & Data: https://cascading-feats.github.io/

</details>


### [126] [Life After Benchmark Saturation: A Case Study of CORE-Bench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26158)
*Nitya Nadgir,Sayash Kapoor,Kangheng Liu,Peter Kirgis,Matilda Orona,Stephan Rabanser,Tilman Bayer,Abhishek Shetty,Yue Ling,Derrick Chan-Sew,Rumi Nakagawa,Saiteja Utpala,Zachary S. Siegel,Arvind Narayanan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出在基准测试准确率饱和后，不应仅关注准确率，而应评估智能体的六个关键维度（构造效度、泛化性、效率、可靠性、模型与脚手架的相对重要性、人机协作提升）。以CORE-Bench Hard为例，展示了这些维度在准确率饱和后仍能提供有意义的洞察，并提出了改进版本CORE-Bench v1.1和OOD任务集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试在准确率饱和后通常被简单替换为更难版本，这忽视了准确率之外的其他重要评估维度，导致对智能体性能的理解不全面。

Method: 以CORE-Bench Hard为案例，系统测量了六个关键维度：识别构造效度威胁（shortcuts等）、引入新基准CORE-Bench v1.1和OOD任务集、测量效率与可靠性、分离模型与脚手架贡献、通过小规模随机实验评估人机协作的效能提升。

Result: 1. 在CORE-Bench Hard中发现了先前难以预见的构造效度威胁；2. 准确率饱和后，基准仍可用于评估效率、可靠性、模型性能和脚手架性能；3. 人机协作在真实计算可重复性任务上实现了约两倍的显著加速（可能被低估，因为五分之一的人类单独复现未完成）。

Conclusion: 研究提出了一种超越准确率中心的更严格的评估范式，通过多维度评估能在准确率饱和后仍获得有价值的智能体性能洞察。

Abstract: When a benchmark's accuracy saturates, it is often retired and replaced with a more challenging version. We show that this approach privileges accuracy and misses the opportunity to study six other key dimensions of agent performance: construct validity issues such as shortcuts, out-of-distribution generalizability, efficiency, reliability, the relative importance of the model versus the scaffold, and uplift from human-agent collaboration. We use CORE-Bench Hard, a benchmark for computational reproducibility of scientific code, as a case study to demonstrate that measuring agents along these dimensions yields meaningful insights into agent performance even after accuracy saturates. First, we surface threats to construct validity in CORE-Bench Hard that are difficult to anticipate with less capable agents. We introduce an improved benchmark, CORE-Bench v1.1, and an out-of-distribution task suite, CORE-Bench OOD. Second, we find that despite accuracy saturation, CORE-Bench v1.1 remains useful for measuring efficiency, reliability, model performance, and scaffold performance. Finally, we conduct a small-scale randomized experiment to measure uplift from human-agent collaboration on real-world computational reproducibility tasks. We find a statistically significant speedup by about a factor of two -- likely underestimated due to one-fifth of human-only reproductions reaching the time limit before completing -- and describe various other findings. Together, our contributions present a more rigorous alternative to the dominant accuracy-centric evaluation paradigm.

</details>


### [127] [Refusal Lives Downstream of Persona in Chat Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26161)
*Viola Zhong,Qirui Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文发现指令微调模型中的拒绝方向与人格方向存在交互：顺从的人格方向会抑制拒绝行为，拒绝方向仅在特定层（后期层）起作用，且取决于人格方向的"门控"作用。单独将拒绝视为一个孤立方向会忽略其对人格的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究分别识别了激活空间中的拒绝方向和人格方向，但两者被视为独立机制。作者想探究它们是否相互作用。

Method: 在Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct和Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct中提取顺从人格方向和拒绝方向，对两者进行干预（steering/projecting），观察在不同层的效果。

Result: 顺从人格方向干预使Llama的拒绝率从97%降到2%；在后期层重新引入拒绝方向可部分恢复拒绝，但前期层不行；在后期层投影掉人格方向可将拒绝率恢复到基线，随机方向则不能。

Conclusion: 拒绝行为在后期表达阶段受到人格方向的门控，拒绝并非独立的方向，其有效性依赖于人格方向的上下文。

Abstract: Linear directions in activation space have been identified for both refusal and persona traits in instruction-tuned chat models, but the two have been studied as separate mechanisms. We show they interact: a compliant persona gates refusal. In Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, we extract a compliant model-persona direction and a refusal direction and intervene on both. Compliant persona steering suppresses refusal -- in Llama, the refusal rate falls from 97% to 2%. Reintroducing the refusal direction partially restores refusal at late layers but not at early ones. Projecting out the persona direction in a late-layer window restores it to baseline; projecting out a random direction does not. Refusal is therefore gated at the late-layer expression stage, downstream of where it is computed. Treating refusal as a single isolated direction misses its dependence on persona.

</details>


### [128] [AlgoEvolve: LLM-driven Meta-evolution of Algorithmic Trading Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26173)
*Dhruv Sharma,Gautam Shroff*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了AlgoEvolve框架，利用LLM作为语义变异算子，通过进化算法自动生成和优化算法交易策略，并引入元进化外循环自动优化提示词，在噪声、非平稳的金融环境中取得了优于人工设计策略的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM驱动的语义进化主要应用于静态编程基准测试，尚未在算法交易这一噪声大、非平稳、高度不连续的复杂动态环境中得到验证。

Method: 提出AlgoEvolve框架：内循环利用LLM作为语义变异算子进化生成Python交易策略，并通过严格测试协议评估；外循环（元进化）进化用于指导内循环程序合成的提示词，自动发现更优的搜索启发式。

Result: 系统展现出涌现性的自适应策略逻辑，能够自主切换交易规则；元进化发现的搜索启发式在探索-利用平衡和减少零交易失败方面一致优于人工设计的指令。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的语义进化为复杂环境下的持续程序合成提供了一种可行方法。

Abstract: Recent work shows that Large Language Models (LLMs) can act as semantic mutation operators for the evolutionary discovery of programs and proofs. Most current applications focus on static coding benchmarks. We extend this paradigm to algorithmic trading. This domain is uniquely challenging because it is noisy, non-stationary, and highly discontinuous. We present AlgoEvolve, an LLM-driven evolutionary framework that generates, evaluates, and iteratively improves executable trading strategies. These strategies are expressed as Python code and evaluated through a rigorous testing protocol. Across multiple experiments, the system exhibits emergent regime-adaptive strategy logic, including autonomous shifts in trading rules. We further introduce a meta-evolutionary outer loop that evolves the prompts guiding program synthesis in the inner loop. This outer loop discovers improved search heuristics. These heuristics balance exploration and exploitation while reducing zero-trade failures. They consistently outperform initial human-designed instructions. The results demonstrate that LLM-based semantic evolution provides a viable approach for continual program synthesis in complex environments.

### [130] [Knowledge-augmented Agentic AI for Mental Health Medication Information Seeking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26205)
*Huizi Yu,Jian Liu,Wenkong Wang,Lingyao Li,Jiayan Zhou,Zhaoqian Xue,Xiang Li,Xinxin Lin,Zhiying Liang,Zhuoru Wu,Siyuan Ma,Xin Ma,Lizhou Fan*

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个基于知识图谱的多智能体框架，整合了Reddit帖子、WebMD评论和FDA不良事件报告系统（FAERS）中九种抗抑郁药的数据。通过大语言模型实体识别管线，发现患者生成的数据（社区平台）与监管报告数据之间存在显著差异，且社区平台能更早发现不良反应信号。框架使用Neo4j知识图谱并保留数据来源，确保可追溯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 患者在线获取药物信息的需求日益增长，但精神科药物的安全性知识分散在权威但抽象的监管不良事件记录和贴近经验但未经验证的患者叙述中。整合这些信息而不混淆证据与轶事在精神病学领域尤为重要，因为信息缺乏上下文会放大恐惧、引发反安慰剂效应并导致治疗不依从。

Method: 开发了一个来源感知的、基于知识图谱的多智能体框架，统一了466,525条Reddit帖子、60,782条WebMD评论以及二十年的FAERS数据，涵盖九种抗抑郁药。使用大语言模型实体识别管线（经医生标注基准测试），采用ATC-N、ICD-10和MedDRA词汇体系，基于Neo4j构建知识图谱以保留数据来源。

Result: 实体识别管线在药物和疾病识别上分别达到0.969和0.973的最高F1分数。两个社区平台之间的一致性（Jaccard相似度高达0.905）远高于与监管报告的一致性，表明患者生成的数据构成了部分独立的安全信号。对于舍曲林，许多不良事件在社区来源中出现的时间比FDA记录早数百天。

Conclusion: 建立了来源感知的整合方法，为更可审计的精神科药物信息提供了可行路径。研究结果表明，患者生成数据与监管数据作为互补而非替代的关系，未来需在前瞻性研究中验证其实用性和患者获益。

Abstract: Patients increasingly seek medication information online, yet safety knowledge for psychiatric drugs is split between regulatory adverse-event records, which are authoritative but abstract, and patient narratives, which are experience-near but unvalidated. Integrating them without conflating evidence and anecdote is especially consequential in psychiatry, where poorly contextualised information can amplify fear, nocebo responses, and non-adherence. Here we develop a provenance-aware, knowledge-graph-based multi-agent framework unifying 466,525 Reddit posts, 60,782 WebMD reviews, and twenty years of U.S. FDA Adverse Event Reporting System records for nine antidepressants. A large-language-model entity-recognition pipeline benchmarked against physician annotations reached highest F1 scores of 0.969 for medications and 0.973 for conditions. The two community platforms were far more concordant with each other (overlap up to a Jaccard similarity of 0.905) than with regulatory reports, indicating that patient-generated data form a partly independent safety signal. For sertraline, many adverse events appeared in community sources hundreds of days before the corresponding FDA date. A Neo4j knowledge graph grounded in ATC-N, ICD-10, and MedDRA vocabularies preserves provenance, keeping every claim traceable and regulatory facts distinct from patient experience. These results establish source-aware integration as a route to more auditable psychiatric medication information, with usefulness and patient benefit to be tested prospectively.

Method: 借鉴认知神经科学中的漂移扩散模型（DDM），将技能表达建模为决策过程，将每一步棋的数据融入评分调整中，并给出严格的数学推导保证DD-Elo与传统Elo系统的偏差有界。

By modeling skill expression as a decision-making process, our model integrates move-level data to capture rapid skill fluctuations. We provide a rigorous mathematical derivation proving that DD-Elo maintains a bounded deviation from the traditional Elo system, ensuring theoretical alignment. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DD-Elo adapts to skill changes faster than Elo. Our findings suggest that DD-Elo offers an explainable, highly responsive, and backward-compatible solution for chess rating ecosystems. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主AI代理可能执行不可逆的高风险行动（如临床开药、软件部署），现有方法过度关注监控推理过程，而非在行动点建立可信约束。

Method: 借鉴人类机构治理自主行动者的模式，提出计算治理模型：智能体保留规划/推理自主权，但高风险行动的执行权被剥离；执行需满足前置条件——每个条件由独立权威源认证、加密绑定到声明意图，并由确定性策略评估；决策记录于防篡改日志中。

Conclusion: 通过"分离推理与执行权+多方独立认证+确定性策略+可审计日志"的架构，可以在不牺牲AI自主性的前提下，对高风险行动施加可验证、可问责的治理约束。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents may begin to perform consequential, irreversible actions such as clinical prescribing and production software deployment. This paper observes that human institutions have governed powerful autonomous actors not by monitoring their reasoning but by requiring independently attested evidence at the point of consequential action. We formalise this institutional pattern as a computational governance model for AI agent systems. Under the proposed model, an agent retains full autonomy over planning and reasoning but holds no execution authority over designated high-risk actions. Execution is conditional on preconditions that are each independently attested by a separate authoritative source, cryptographically bound to a declared intent, and evaluated by a deterministic policy. Decisions are recorded in a tamper-evident log amenable to independent re-verification. We present a proof-of-concept implementation and illustrate the model with examples from software deployment and clinical prescribing.

Our system acts as a highly effective collaborative assistant, generating structural starting points that human artists can further expand and shape. ### [134] [The Verification Horizon: No Silver Bullet for Coding Agent Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26300)
*Binghai Wang,Chenlong Zhang,Dayiheng Liu,Jiajun Zhang,Jiawei Chen,Mouxiang Chen,Rongyao Fang,Siyuan Zhang,Xuwu Wang,Yuheng Jing,Zeyao Ma,Zeyu Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出在编码智能体中，验证比生成更困难，因为生成方案已变得容易而可靠验证却难以实现。作者从可扩展性、保真度和鲁棒性三个维度刻画验证信号质量，研究了四种奖励构建方式，并指出没有固定奖励函数能随策略能力增长保持有效，验证必须与生成器共同进化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统直觉认为验证比生成更容易，但在当前编码智能体中这一直觉被颠覆：随着基础模型推理能力增强和工程框架成熟，生成复杂候选方案已不再困难，而可靠验证反而成为更难的问题。每个可构建的验证器都只是人类意图的代理，而非意图本身，导致验证面临双重困难：意图本身天然欠指定，以及优化过程会扩大代理与意图之间的差距（表现为奖励破解或信号饱和）。

Method: 从三个维度（可扩展性、保真度、鲁棒性）刻画验证信号质量，并研究四种奖励构建方式：通用编码任务的测试验证器、前端任务的评分标准验证器、真实世界智能体任务中以用户作为验证器、长周期任务中的自动化智能体验证器。在不同任务类型和策略能力水平下进行深入分析和实验。

Result: 针对性验证设计能有效抑制奖励破解，提高任务完成质量，在多个内部和公共基准上取得显著提升。

Conclusion: 没有固定奖励函数能随策略能力持续增长而保持有效，验证必须与生成器共同进化。验证信号质量的核心挑战在于同时实现可扩展性、保真度和鲁棒性三者。

Abstract: A classical intuition holds that verifying a solution is easier than producing one. For today's coding agents, this intuition is being inverted: as foundation models develop stronger reasoning capabilities and engineering harnesses grow more sophisticated, generating complex candidate solutions is no longer difficult -- reliably verifying them has become the harder problem. Every verifier we can build is only a proxy for human intent, never the intent itself. This makes verification subject to a twofold difficulty: first, intent is underspecified by nature, making it inherently hard to faithfully check whether it has been fulfilled; second, during model training, optimization widens the gap between proxy and intent -- manifesting as reward hacking or signal saturation. To address this, we characterize the quality of verification signals along three dimensions -- scalability, faithfulness, and robustness -- and argue that achieving all three simultaneously is the central challenge. We further study four reward constructions: a test verifier for general coding tasks, a rubric verifier for frontend tasks, the user as verifier for real-world agent tasks, and an automated agent verifier for long-horizon tasks. Across different task types and policy capability levels, we conduct in-depth analysis and experiments on the core challenges of reward design and how to more effectively leverage reward signals. Experiments show that targeted verification design can effectively suppress reward hacking, improve task completion quality, and achieve significant gains across multiple internal and public benchmarks. These experiences collectively point to a core observation: no fixed reward function can remain effective as policy capability continues to grow; and verification must co-evolve with the generator.

A realistic depot case study evaluates day-ahead and real-time operations under profit-based and operation-based coordination modes, considering service delays, route-energy deviations, electricity price shocks, and combined disturbances. The results show that agentic aggregation can support adaptive fleet-grid coordination by maintaining feasible schedules, activating re-optimization selectively, and improving the use of charging and V2G flexibility. However, they also reveal a critical trade-off: the same agentic capability that reduces operational complexity can extract value from the PTO when configured around profit-oriented pricing. These findings suggest that agentic aggregators can become useful for managing electric bus V2G operations, but their deployment in public-fleet contexts requires transparent coordination modes, auditable tariff-setting, and explicit value-sharing rules.

This is a critical gap for a sector that requires live data retrieval, specialized regulatory and market knowledge, and multi-step quantitative reasoning under real-world constraints.
  We present an empirical study of tool-augmented LLM agents on real-world energy market analytics tasks. Our evaluation environment includes 243 expert-curated problems across three categories: (1) Market Data Retrieval and Analysis, (2) Knowledge Retrieval and Interpretation, and (3) Advanced Quantitative Modeling and Decision Analytics. Tasks include price and demand analysis, tariff impact modeling, asset revenue and returns estimation, hedging strategy analysis, and optimization modeling, with problems spanning multiple difficulty levels.
  Agents are equipped with a configurable suite of domain tools, including live electricity market APIs for major U.S. ISOs, regulatory docket search, utility tariff databases, asset optimization models, and retrieval-augmented generation over energy market documents. We assess agent responses using a multi-dimensional evaluation protocol that scores approach correctness, answer accuracy, attribute alignment, and source validity, with category-aware routing to match scoring criteria to question type. We evaluate both closed-source and open-source LLMs, providing a comparative analysis of how model capability and domain tooling interact in a high-stakes professional domain. Key artifacts are publicly released to support reproducibility and future research.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出叙事式思维（NoT）系统提示，将思维链强制分为五个部分：主角、利益相关者、两步后果、不确定性、承诺。无需额外训练、参数调整或微调。进一步使用文本梯度下降优化提示，并扩展为五轮多利益相关者辩论协议。

Abstract: Standard chain-of-thought on moral dilemmas exhibits two failure modes: stakeholder collapse (the trace names at most one party with a stake in the outcome) and uncertainty suppression (no explicit unknowns or hedges before committing to an action). We introduce narration-of-thought (NoT), a system prompt that structures chain-of-thought into five sections: protagonist, stakeholders, two-step consequences, uncertainty, then commitment. NoT adds no training, parameters, or fine-tuning. On 100 DailyDilemmas scenarios across four generators from three vendors, NoT cuts stakeholder collapse from up to 31% to under 1% and uncertainty suppression from up to 72% to 1-24% on every model. Extended to a five-round multi-stakeholder debate protocol, the scaffold converts a 6% standoff into 95% full consensus on a calibration set and 100% combined convergence on a DailyDilemmas replication. ### [140] [Instruction Bleed: Cross-Module Interference in Prompt-Composed Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26356)
*Ching-Yu Lin,Yifan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了组合行为泄露（CBL）现象：即使没有共享变量或可执行依赖，编辑一个提示模块会静默改变其他模块的行为。通过在部署的智能体系统（Claude Sonnet 4.6, 144次试验）中进行三通道协议实验，发现内容通道产生可检测的成对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63），但未导致推荐翻转——这种亚阈值状态在标准QA中不可见，但在智能体处理数千次决策时会累积。CBL与已知故障类型正交，需要将跨模块干扰测量纳入提示组合智能体评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实践中报告了一个反复出现的故障模式：编辑一个提示模块会无声地改变其他模块的行为，即使它们之间没有共享变量或可执行依赖。这种干扰未被系统研究或形式化定义，需要建立一个可操作的框架来识别和测量这种跨模块干扰。

Method: 形式化定义了 compositional behavioral leakage (CBL)，基于Transformer自注意力的非隔离特性。设计了可复用的三通道协议（volume/content/form），在部署的作业评估智能体（Claude Sonnet 4.6）上进行144次试验，通过扰动非焦点模块来检测行为泄露。

Result: 只有内容通道产生了可检测的成对效应（Cohen's d = 0.63，bootstrap 95% CI排除零），但未导致推荐翻转。CBL与对抗注入、认知退化、多智能体故障传播、隐私泄露等已知故障轴线正交。

Conclusion: CBL是一种新的、未被充分认识的故障类型，其影响在常规QA测试中不可见，但在智能体系统长期运行中会累积。需要将跨模块干扰测量作为提示组合智能体评估的必要组成部分。贡献包括：操作定义、可复用协议、可证伪的预测集和系统类特征描述。

Abstract: Practitioners of prompt-composed agentic systems report a recurring failure mode: editing one prompt module silently shifts the behavior of others despite no shared variable or executable dependency. We formalize this as compositional behavioral leakage (CBL): interference between modules sharing a context window. CBL is enabled by architectural non-isolation: transformer self-attention provides no formal boundary between concatenated modules. We probe CBL on a deployed job-evaluation agent (Claude Sonnet 4.6, 144 trials) through a reusable three-channel protocol that perturbs non-focal modules along volume, content, and form. Only the content channel produces a detectable paired effect (Cohen's d = 0.63, bootstrap 95% CI excluding zero); no recommendation flipped -- a sub-threshold regime invisible to standard QA but compounding across the thousands of decisions a deployed agent makes. CBL is orthogonal to known agent-failure axes (adversarial injection, cognitive degradation, multi-agent fault propagation, privacy leakage). We contribute an operational definition, a reusable protocol, a falsifiable prediction set, and a system-class characterization, establishing cross-module interference measurement as a requirement for prompt-composed agent evaluation.

### [141] [Accelerating Returns and the Qualitative Engine for Science](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26359)
*Guojun Liao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对Kurzweil的加速回报理论进行数学解释，指出该理论主要适用于执行和基础设施能力，而非科学发现中的定性推理能力。通过ARC-AGI-3基准测试（人类接近完美，AI低于1%）说明当前AI与人类灵活推理的巨大差距，并引入"科学定性引擎（QES）"作为补充方案，强调科学发现过程本身就是值得保存的人类智慧。

Method: 论文采用理论分析方法：首先对加速回报理论给出简化的数学解释；然后通过ARC-AGI-3基准测试的人类-AI性能对比（人类接近100%，AI<1%）作为实证锚点，区分"执行加速"与"发现推理"两种不同能力；最后引入QES框架作为解决定性推理缺失的方案。

Result: 论证了即使加速回报理论成立，它也只能解释量化计算能力的指数增长，而无法解决科学发现中最关键的结构性框架转换问题。ARC-AGI-3的极端性能差距（人类与AI之间）有力地支持了这一区分。

Conclusion: 科学发现过程本身是一种值得保存的人类智慧形式，QES的价值不依赖于AGI何时到来，而在于它系统性地组织和传承科学发现中的定性推理能力——这是Kurzweil式加速无法覆盖的领域。

Abstract: Ray Kurzweil described a thesis of accelerating returns, which is the most influential narratives in discussions of technological progress. Its central claim is that advances in multiple technological fields, especially compute, artificial intelligence, brain science, and biotechnology, interact in such a way that progress becomes self-amplifying and approximately exponential. This paper gives a simple mathematical interpretation of that claim and then argues that, even if such acceleration is real, it does not by itself resolve the central problem of scientific discovery. The reason is that accelerating returns apply most naturally to executional and infrastructural capability, whereas genuine discovery often depends on a different capacity: qualitative reasoning about when a current framework is structurally inadequate and what conceptual move is needed next. Recent ARC-AGI-3 results sharpen this distinction: humans solve the benchmark at ceiling, whereas frontier AI systems remain below 1%, indicating that the gap between current AI and human flexible reasoning is still very large. At the same time, Demis Hassabis has emphasized that humans must retain their sense of meaning and what they choose to focus their lives on, a reminder that the future of AI is not only a technical forecast but also a question of what forms of human understanding are worth preserving and transmitting. This paper positions the Qualitative Engine for Science (QES) [3] as a response to that missing capacity. In this view, the Kurzweil theory helps explain why quantitative capability may accelerate, while QES addresses the central problem in scientific discovery that acceleration alone does not solve. Its value does not depend on when AGI arrives, but on the fact that the processes of scientific discovery themselves constitute a form of human wisdom worth preserving, organizing, and making accessible.

### [142] [Geometry-Aware MCTS for Extremal Problems in Combinatorial Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26399)
*Luoning Zhang,Xu Zhuang,Tianhao Wang,Nathan Kaplan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种几何感知的蒙特卡洛树搜索（Geometry-Aware MCTS）框架，用于解决组合几何中的极值问题（如No-Three-in-Line问题），通过增量约束检查、几何对称性剪枝和批量对称转移策略，在六个问题中的五个上取得了新的最佳计算结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合几何中的极值问题（如n×n网格上的点配置）面临严格的全局几何约束，传统精确求解器存在组合爆炸问题，标准强化学习和Transformer模型则受限于稀疏奖励陷阱和二次规模的token消耗限制，亟需一种高效且可扩展的求解方法。

Method: 提出Geometry-Aware MCTS框架，核心包括：(1) 增量更新可行动作空间，严格强制执行几何约束，将共线点检查复杂度从O(n³)降至O(n²)；(2) 利用几何对称性进行节点扩展时的规范剪枝以减小分支因子；(3) 采用对称批量转移加速发现优质配置。

Result: 在六个问题中的五个上取得了新的最佳计算结果。对于Max-N3IL问题，在82≤n≤119的网格上获得了约1.8n的配置规模；对于Smallest Complete Set问题，在测试网格上获得约0.95n的配置规模，提供了新的上界。

Conclusion: Geometry-Aware MCTS是一种高度适应性的框架，能够有效发现组合几何中的新配置，为解决复杂几何约束下的极值问题提供了新的有效途径。

Abstract: We study certain extremal problems in combinatorial geometry that ask about configurations of points in an $n \times n$ grid that satisfy strict, global geometric constraints. Classical exact solvers suffer from combinatorial explosion for these types of problems, and standard reinforcement learning and transformer-based models struggle with the sparse reward "validity cliff" and quadratic token-consumption limits. To overcome these bottlenecks, we propose a Geometry-Aware Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) framework. Our approach strictly enforces geometric constraints through incremental updates to the feasible action space. For constraints about collections of collinear points, like those that occur in the classic No-Three-in-Line problem (Max-N3IL), this mechanism reduces the constraint checking complexity from $O(n^3)$ to $O(n^2)$. To improve search efficiency, we exploit geometric symmetries in two ways: canonical pruning during node expansion to reduce the branching factor, and symmetric batch transitions to accelerate the discovery of promising configurations. We perform extensive experiments and establish new best-known computational results on five out of six of the problems that we considered. Notably, for Max-N3IL we find configurations of size roughly $1.8 n$ for grids of size $82 \le n \le 119$. For the Smallest Complete Set problem, we find configurations of size roughly $0.95 n$, providing new upper bounds within the tested grids. This work establishes Geometry-Aware MCTS as a highly adaptable framework for discovering novel configurations in combinatorial geometry.

### [143] [Unbiased Canonical Set-Valued Oracles Via Lattice Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26418)
*Jobst Heitzig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种避免自指悖论的概率预测框架：通过Knaster-Tarski不动点定理构造自洽的credal set（信念集），取代传统的单点概率估计，解决了"预言机"在知晓自身预测会影响事件概率时的根本性矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非具身AI（"预言机"）在预测未来事件概率时面临自指问题：一旦其答案被知晓并采取行动，就会改变它原本被要求报告的概率。已有方案（如Scientist AI）主张只回答反事实问题（即假设答案无影响），但这类答案在被告知后因其前提失效而变得无关紧要。因此需要一种自指代替代方案。

Method: 提出预言机不报告单点概率，而是报告一个credal set（信念集），该集合同时满足无偏性和自洽性（即与被告知后的后果一致）。利用Knaster-Tarski不动点定理，在封闭credal集的完全格上取一个适当地定义 isotone 算子的最小不动点；另一种变体则报告包含所有自洽点估计的最小不动点。该构造基于纯格论，可从二元事件B自然推广到任意随机变量X。

Result: 证明了存在性、自洽性和非空性；证明了对非表演性（non-performative）问题，该构造退化为经典点估计；对二元事件，在自然凸包分解假设下，规范答案是一个区间。该构造可从二元事件B无条件推广到任意随机变量X的条件律。

Conclusion: 提出的credal set框架成功地解决了概率预测的自指悖论，给出了一个既有理论保证又有规范性的解。结论指出该构造是纯格论的，可推广到一般随机变量。开放问题包括区间特征化在推广后是否仍然成立。

Abstract: A non-agentic "oracle" AI that estimates probabilities of future events faces a self-reference problem: once its answer is learned and acted upon, it can change the very probability it was asked to report. One response, advocated for the Scientist AI programme, is to ask only counterfactual questions, evaluated as if the answer had no influence. We observe that such answers tend to become irrelevant the moment they are learned, precisely because their premise is then false. We therefore explore a self-referential alternative in which the oracle reports not a single probability but a credal set that is simultaneously unbiased and self-consistent with the consequences of being learned. The naive self-consistency requirement is satisfied by too many sets (including the useless answer $[0,1]$), so the problem is to single out a canonical, nontrivial member. We do so with the Knaster--Tarski fixed-point theorem on the complete lattice of closed credal sets, taking the least fixed point of a suitably defined isotone operator; a variant instead reports the least fixed point that contains every self-consistent point estimate. We prove existence, self-consistency, and nonemptiness, show that the construction collapses to the classical point answer for non-performative questions, and that for a binary event the canonical answer is, under a natural hull-factoring assumption, an interval. The development is purely lattice-theoretic and extends unchanged from a binary event $B$ to an arbitrary random variable $X$, with $P(B\mid A,C)$ replaced by the conditional law $\mathcal{L}(X\mid A,C)$. We close with open questions, including whether the interval characterization itself survives that generalization.

</details>


### [144] [Estimating Uncertainty in Classifier Performance with Applications to Large Language Models and Nested Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26422)
*Kylie Anglin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了在社会科学文本分类情境下（小样本、低频构念、嵌套文本）不同置信区间方法对性能指标的准确性，发现Wald区间和基础百分位自助法最不准确，而Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson及一种新颖的伪计数正则化自助法表现更优，并强调嵌套数据需调整有效样本量和自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前研究在使用文本分类（监督模型或大语言模型）测量构念时，虽然报告召回率和精确率等指标作为效度证据，但这些点估计存在抽样变异性，而置信区间报告却 inconsistently。此外，当标注数据集较小或性能较高时，现有区间估计方法往往不适用。因此需要系统评估适合社会科学文本分类条件的置信区间方法。

Method: 通过模拟实验，在社会科学文本分类的典型条件下（小到中等样本量、低频构念、文本嵌套在个体内）评估多种置信区间方法，包括Wald区间、Agresti-Coull区间、Wilson区间、Clopper-Pearson区间、基础百分位自助法、以及提出的新颖伪计数正则化自助法（特别针对F1）。同时评估嵌套数据下的层次自助法和聚类自助法。

Result: Wald区间和基础百分位自助法准确性最差，覆盖率有时远低于名义95%水平。Agresti-Coull、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson和提出的伪计数正则化自助法准确性更高。在嵌套文本情境下，层次自助法在个体产生中等数量文本时更准确，但在个体仅产生少量文本时过于保守；分析性区间需要对有效N和适当自由度进行调整。

Conclusion: 本文为社会科学文本分类提供了置信区间选择的指导，旨在提高机器学习应用的透明度，并鼓励在研究设计阶段更加关注验证样本量。

Abstract: Researchers increasingly use text classification--supervised models or large language models--to measure constructs from natural language, providing metrics such as recall and precision as evidence of their validity. Yet, though these metrics are point estimates subject to sampling variation, measures of uncertainty are inconsistently reported alongside them. Further, when they are reported, they are often estimated with methods that are not appropriate when relevant labelled datasets are small or performance is high. To increase and improve confidence interval reporting in the field, this paper evaluates confidence interval methods for performance metrics under conditions typical of social science text classification: small to moderate sample sizes, infrequent constructs, and texts nested within individuals. Across simulations, default methods such as the Wald interval and the basic percentile bootstrap are the least accurate, with coverage sometimes far below the nominal 95% level. Accuracy is improved with the use of Agresti-Coull, Wilson, Clopper-Pearson, and a novel pseudo-count regularized bootstrap (which is particularly relevant to the calculation of F1). When texts are nested within individuals, we demonstrate that adjustment for both effective N and the appropriate degrees of freedom is necessary for producing accurate analytic intervals. Among bootstrap intervals, the hierarchical bootstrap is more accurate than the cluster bootstrap when individuals produce a moderate number of texts but overly conservative when individuals produce only a few. By providing guidance to the field on appropriate interval estimation, we aim to improve the transparency of machine learning applications, and to encourage greater attention to the validation sample size at the design stage.

</details>


### [145] [Data-driven Machine Learning Cannot Reach Symbolic-level Logical Reasoning -- The Limit of the Scaling Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26454)
*Tiansi Dong,Mateja Jamnik,Pietro Liò*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文论证了监督深度学习无法达到符号级别三段论推理的严谨性，主要归因于两个方法论限制：训练数据无法区分全部24种有效三段论推理类型，以及端到端映射在模式识别与逻辑推理组件间引入矛盾训练目标。实验表明Euler Net无法实现严谨三段论推理，ChatGPT虽可能达到100%准确率但仍提供错误解释，从而得出结论：监督机器学习系统无法达到符号逻辑推理的严谨水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨数据驱动机器学习系统通过增加训练数据和训练时间，是否能够达到符号级三段论推理的严谨水平，即检验逻辑推理领域是否存在缩放定律的极限。

Method: 理论分析揭示监督深度学习的两项方法论限制（训练数据不完整、组件间矛盾目标）; 实验验证Euler Net在三段论推理中的表现; 测试ChatGPT（GPT-5-nano和GPT-5）在不同表面形式（单词、双词、简单符号、长随机符号）下判断三段论可满足性的能力。

Result: Euler Net无法实现严谨的三段论推理; 表面形式影响ChatGPT推理性能; ChatGPT GPT-5可能达到100%准确率但仍提供错误解释。

Conclusion: 监督机器学习系统无法达到符号逻辑推理的严谨水平，因为经验训练过程在达到100%准确率后便停止，而符号推理需要更深层次的逻辑严谨性。

Abstract: Sphere neural networks have achieved symbolic level syllogistic reasoning without training data, raising the question of where the limit of the scaling law for logical reasoning lies, i.e., whether data-driven machine learning systems can achieve the same level by increasing training data and training time. We show two methodological limitations that prevent supervised deep learning from reaching the symbolic-level syllogistic reasoning: (1) training data can not distinguish all 24 types of valid syllogistic reasoning; (2) end-to-end mapping from premises to conclusion introduces contradictory training targets between neural components for pattern recognition and logical reasoning. Beside theoretical analysis, we experimentally illustrate that Euler Net cannot achieve rigorous syllogistic reasoning. We further challenge the most recent ChatGPTs (GPT-5-nano and GPT-5) to determine the satisfiability of syllogistic statements in four surface forms (patterns): words, double words, simple symbols, and long random symbols, showing that surface forms affect the reasoning performance and that ChatGPT GPT-5 may reach 100% accuracy but still provide incorrect explanations. As empirical training processes are stopped after achieving 100% accuracy, we conclude that supervised machine learning systems will not attain the rigour of symbolic logical reasoning.

*Xiaochen Wang,Bao Hoang,Han Liu,Ting Wang,Fenglong Ma*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) over knowledge graphs has emerged as a promising approach for grounding large language models, yet existing benchmarks largely overlook the challenges of retrieval in multimodal knowledge graph RAG (MKG-RAG). In practice, retrieval is a critical bottleneck: multimodal knowledge is heterogeneous, difficult to align across modalities, and often poorly served by retrievers designed for unstructured corpora. To address this gap, we introduce MKG-RAG-Bench, a cross-domain benchmark explicitly designed to evaluate retrieval in MKG-RAG. MKG-RAG-Bench is constructed from two multimodal knowledge graphs spanning general and medical domains, and includes carefully aligned question-answering datasets that support controlled evaluation of both retrieval and downstream generation. The benchmark is built using an LLM-based curation pipeline that filters low-utility knowledge, generates structurally grounded queries with exact supervision, and systematically covers diverse modality configurations. Through extensive experiments across representative retriever families and modality settings, we show that effective multimodal retrieval remains challenging yet crucial for end-to-end MKG-RAG performance, and that retrieval quality strongly determines generation outcomes. By isolating retrieval as a first-class evaluation target, MKG-RAG-Bench provides a principled foundation for diagnosing current limitations and advancing multimodal knowledge graph RAG systems.

Data collection is a major bottleneck in this pipeline, however. Psychology, and computational cognitive science in particular, is well-positioned to benefit from AI experimentation because theories are often represented as code and crowdsourcing platforms enable programmatic human data collection at scale. Here, we apply automated discovery techniques to the project of generating theories in computational cognitive science, with an agent-based system collecting human data independently through crowdsourced survey experiments. As a testbed, we use a classic case study from cognitive psychology: judging which sequences of coin flips seem subjectively more random. Our system, auto-psych, uses nested agent-based discovery loops to generate explanatory theories of human behavior. The inner loop conjectures, fits, and critiques probabilistic cognitive models; the outer loop designs experiments to test these models, launches them online, and analyzes the data. This system can quickly and reliably recover ground-truth theories from synthetic data via systematic experimentation, but the nested structure is critical to model performance. Further, in three independent sequences of human experiments, the system finds theories that fit the data better than theories generated from the scientific literature. This work thus demonstrates the feasibility of automated data collection and theory discovery in computational cognitive science.

### [149] [Humans Disengage, Reasoning Models Persist: Separating Difficulty Registration from Deliberation Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26502)
*Han-yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型推理模型(LRM)在难题上花费更多token，但有趣的是，对于同一道题，当模型答错时花费的token反而比答对时更多；而人类则相反——答错的题目花费时间更短。这种"跨题目一致但题目内相反"的模式揭示了两者在推理资源分配策略上的根本差异：人类表现为"投入vs放弃"，而LRM表现为"不确定性驱动长度"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然LRM在难题上花更多时间（与人类类似），但这种表面相似性掩盖了题目层面的相反模式。作者旨在区分两种不同层次的推理时间/资源分配机制，并揭示LRM与人类在"如何分配推理资源"上的本质差异。

Method: 在一个公开的人机对照语料库上，比较人类（反应时间）与五种思维链LRM（token数）在两个层面的表现：(1) 跨题目的难度追踪（registration）；(2) 同一题目内，成功与失败时的资源分配（allocation）。使用Cohen's d量化效应量，并控制题目固定效应进行验证。

Result: 人类与所有五种LRM在跨题目层面表现一致（难度越高，资源越多），但在题目内部层面完全相反：LRM在答错时花费更多token（Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13），而人类在答错时花费更少时间。该结果在多个数据集上复现，且非思维链基线上不存在此模式。

Conclusion: 两种策略共享相同的跨题目难度信号，但执行相反的停止策略：人类在预期能解决的题目上持续投入，在没把握时放弃；LRM在不确定时生成更长链，而这恰恰导致失败。这揭示了仅靠跨题目相关性（先前研究常用的指标）无法捕捉到题目内资源分配策略的本质差异。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) take longer on harder problems, just as humans do. This surface similarity hides an opposite pattern within items. When an LRM gets a problem wrong, it spends more tokens than when it gets the same problem right; humans do the reverse, spending less time on the trials they get wrong. We separate two levels of deliberation: how response time tracks difficulty across items (registration), and, with item identity held fixed, whether an agent spends more on its own failures or successes (allocation). On a public matched human-LRM corpus, humans and all five thinking LRMs reproduce the known cross-item alignment (registration) but diverge within items (allocation): every LRM shows a large wrong-vs-right effect (Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13 on H-ARC) while humans show the opposite sign. The comparison stays inside each agent's own scale; we never put seconds and tokens on one axis. The dissociation holds under item fixed effects, replicates across datasets, and is absent in a non-thinking baseline. We read the human pattern as engagement versus abandonment: people stay on items they expect to solve and give up on the rest. We read the LRM pattern as length driven by uncertainty: chains grow when the model is unsure, which is exactly when it tends to fail. Both policies produce the same cross-item correlation with difficulty, so they look aligned on the measure prior work has used; the divergence shows up only once item identity is fixed. Under resource-rational metareasoning, the split is between two stopping policies that share a difficulty signal but implement opposite control; trace length captures the signal and misses the control.

</details>
